country_event = {
	id = fraeco.1
	title = fraeco.1.title
	desc = fraeco.1.desc
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		date > 1936.2.10
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_big_city
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = fraeco.1.a
		add_ideas = DB_FRA_eco_reform1
		add_ideas = DB_FRA_eco_malpractice_industry1
		add_ideas = DB_FRA_eco_malpractice_agriculture1
		add_ideas = DB_FRA_eco_malpractice_innovation1

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = frapoc.907 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = frapha.1
	title = frapha.1.title
	desc = frapha.1.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { Pha_coop_agree = 0 }
		set_variable = { Pha_coop_disagree = 0 }
		set_variable = { Pha_coop_abstain = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = frapha.1.a
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		trigger = {
			FRA = { 
				has_completed_focus = FRA_econ_cop 
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = Pha_eco_coop_level1

					has_country_flag = Pha_eco_coop_level5

			}

		}
		set_country_flag = FRA_pha_discuss_about_eco
		set_country_flag = FRA_pha_coop_eco
		
		hidden_effect = {
			INT_coop_pp_cost = yes 
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { FRA_is_phalanstere_member = yes }
				country_event = frapha.5
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = frapha.5
	title = frapha.5.title
	desc = frapha.5.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		FRA = { INT_coop_pp_cost = yes }
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_political_power < FRA.INT_coop_cost
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { tt = FRA.Pha_disrepect }
				multiply_temp_variable = { tt = -10 }
				add = tt
			}
		}
		name = frapha.5.a
		set_temp_variable = { INT_coop_cost_t = FRA.INT_coop_cost }
		multiply_temp_variable = { INT_coop_cost_t = -1 }
		add_political_power = INT_coop_cost_t
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.pha_coop_agree_tag 
			value = THIS
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { tt = FRA.Pha_disrepect }
				multiply_temp_variable = { tt = 10 }
				add = tt
			}
		}
		name = frapha.5.b
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.pha_coop_disagree_tag 
			value = THIS
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_political_power < 25
			}
		}
		name = frapha.5.c
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.pha_coop_abstain_tag 
			value = THIS
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = frapha.8
	title = frapha.8.title
	desc = frapha.8.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = frapha.8.a
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				0 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 1
						FRA = { 
							has_completed_focus = FRA_econ_cop 
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = Pha_eco_coop_level1
								has_country_flag = Pha_eco_coop_level2
								has_country_flag = Pha_eco_coop_level3
								has_country_flag = Pha_eco_coop_level4
								has_country_flag = Pha_eco_coop_level5
							}
						}
						check_variable = { Pha_completed_tech_coop < 8 }
					}
					set_country_flag = FRA_pha_discuss_about_eco
					set_country_flag = FRA_pha_coop_eco
				}
				0 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 1
						FRA = { 
							has_completed_focus = FRA_techn_cop 
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = Pha_tech_coop_level1
								has_country_flag = Pha_tech_coop_level2
								has_country_flag = Pha_tech_coop_level3
								has_country_flag = Pha_tech_coop_level4

						region = 130

			limit = {

					specialization = specialization_nuclear
					level > 0
				}

				specialization = specialization_nuclear
				level = 3
			}

			add_building_construction = {

				level = 1

			set_technology = { atomic_research = 1 }

			limit = {
				NOT = { is_special_project_completed = sp:sp_nuclear_reactor }
			}
			complete_special_project = sp:sp_nuclear_reactor
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_special_project_completed = sp:sp_nuclear_bomb }
			}

		set_temp_variable = { at = sore_yout_accept }

		multiply_temp_variable = { at = 0.01 }

		multiply_temp_variable = { typhon_stability_factor = -0.4 }

		multiply_temp_variable = { typhon_political_power_factor = 0.5 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { typhon_political_power_factor = -0.4 }

		set_temp_variable = { typhon_army_attack_factor = qt }
		multiply_temp_variable = { typhon_army_attack_factor = 0.25 }
		set_temp_variable = { typhon_army_defence_factor = qt }
		multiply_temp_variable = { typhon_army_defence_factor = 0.25 }

		set_temp_variable = { typhon_production_speed_nuclear_reactor_factor = qt }
		multiply_temp_variable = { typhon_production_speed_nuclear_reactor_factor = 0.5 }

		set_temp_variable = { typhon_nuclear_production_factor = qt }
		multiply_temp_variable = { typhon_nuclear_production_factor = 0.5 }

		set_temp_variable = { typhon_terrain_penalty_reduction = qt }
		multiply_temp_variable = { typhon_terrain_penalty_reduction = 0.3 }
